});\n   165‚Üí    \n   166‚Üí    try {\n   167‚Üí      const aiModule = await import('@/lib/ai-stage-runner');\n   168‚Üí      const loadTime = Date.now() - startTime;\n   169‚Üí      \n   170‚Üí    \n   187‚Üí      console.log('[WizardShell] ‚úÖ AI stage runner function validated successfully');\n   188‚Üí      \n   189‚Üí    } catch (error: any) {\n   190‚Üí      const loadTime = Date.now() - startTime;\n   191‚Üí      const errorDetails = {\n   192‚Üí        loadTimeMs: loadTime,\n   193‚Üí        attempt: retryAttempt + 1,\n   194‚Üí        errorMessage: error.message,\n   195‚Üí \n   204‚Üí      console.error('[WizardShell] ‚ùå Failed to load AI stage runner:', errorDetails);\n   205‚Üí      \n   206‚Üí      setAiLoadAttempts(retryAttempt + 1);\n   207‚Üí      setAiLoadError(error.message);\n   208‚Üí      \n   209‚Üí      // Auto-retry up to 3 times with exponential backoff\n   210‚Üí      if (retryAttempt < 2) {\n   211‚Üí        const retryDelay =    } else {\n   220‚Üí        // Final failure - show comprehensive error toast\n   221‚Üí        const comprehensiveError = `AI Module Load Failed After ${retryAttempt + 1} Attempts\n   222‚Üí\n   223‚Üíüîç Technical Details:\n   224‚Üí‚Ä¢ Error: ${error.message}\n   225‚Üí‚Ä¢ Load time: ${loadTime}ms\n   226‚Üí‚Ä¢ Network: ${navigator.onLine ?              setAiStageLoaded(false);\n   251‚Üí                setAiLoadError(null);\n   252‚Üí                setAiLoadAttempts(0);\n   253‚Üí                loadAiStageRunner();\n   254‚Üí              }}\n   255‚Üí              size=\"sm\"\n   256‚Üí            >\n   257‚Üí              Retry\n   258‚Üí            </Button>\n   259‚Üí          )\n   260‚Üí        });\n   261‚Üí      }\n 297‚Üí    updateInstance: updateInstanceForPersistence,\n   298‚Üí  });\n   299‚Üí\n   300‚Üí  const updateStageState = useCallback((stageId: string, updates: Partial<StageState>) => {\n   301‚Üí 321‚Üí\n   322‚Üí    if (needsImmediateSave) {\n   323‚Üí      // Next tick save so React state has committed\n   324‚Üí      setTimeout(() => {\n   325‚Üí        saveDocument();\n   326‚Üí      }, (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   332‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   333‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   334‚Üí\n   335‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   336‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   337‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized correctly\n   338‚Üí\n   339‚Üí      // Evaluate basic dependencies\n   340‚Üí      let depsMet = true;\n   341‚Üí      if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   342‚Üí        depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   343‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   344‚Üí        );\n   345‚Üí      }\n   346‚Üí\n   347‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   348‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   349‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   350‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   351‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   352‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   353‚Üí          );\n   354‚Üí        }\n   355‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   356‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   357‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   358‚Üí          );\n   359‚Üí        }\n   360‚Üí      }\n   361‚Üí      \n   362‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   363‚Üí      if (currentState.status === 'completed' && currentState.output && currentState.completedAt) {\n   364‚Üí        // ONLY check staleness for truly completed stages\n   365‚Üí        const stageCompletedAt = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   366‚Üí        \n   367‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   368‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   369‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   370‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   371‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   372‚Üí          });\n   373‚Üí        }\n   374‚Üí        \n   375‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   376‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   377‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   378‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   379‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   380‚Üí          });\n   381‚Üí        }\n   382‚Üí        \n   383‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   384‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   385‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   386‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   387‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   388‚Üí          });\n   389‚Üí        }\n   390‚Üí      }\n   391‚Üí\n   392‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   393‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   394‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   395‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   396‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   397‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   398‚Üí        );\n   399‚Üí      } else {\n   400‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   401‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   402‚Üí      }\n   403‚Üí\n   404‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   405‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   406‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   407‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   408‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   409‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   410‚Üí        } else {\n   411‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   412‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   413‚Üí        }\n   414‚Üí      }\n   415‚Üí\n   416‚Üí      if (\n   417‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   418‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   419‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   420‚Üí      ) {\n   421‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   422‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   423‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   424‚Üí          isStale: isStale,\n   425‚Üí          shouldAutoRun: shouldAutoRun,\n   426‚Üí          // Reset staleDismissed when stage is no longer stale\n   427‚Üí          staleDismissed: isStale ? currentState.staleDismissed : false,\n   428‚Üí        };\n   429‚Üí        changed = true;\n   430‚Üí      }\n   431‚Üí    });\n   432‚Üí    return changed ? newStageStates : currentStageStates; // Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   433‚Üí  };\n   434‚Üí  \n   435‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   436‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   437‚Üí 441‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   442‚Üí\n   443‚Üí\n   444‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   445‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   446‚Üí      const stageState = instance.stageStates[stage.id];\n   447‚Üí      // Defensive check: ensure stageState exists before accessing its properties\n   448‚Üí      if (stageState && }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   455‚Üí\n   456‚Üí\n   457‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   458‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n   459‚Üí    if (titleStageId) {\n   460‚Üí      const titleStageState = instance.stageStates[titleStageId];\n   461‚Üí      if (titleStageState?.status === 'completed' && titleStageState.output) {\n 495‚Üí\n   496‚Üí\n   497‚Üí  const handleInputChange = (stageId: string, fieldName: string, value: any) => {\n   498‚Üí    // This is primarily for simple input types like 'textarea' or 'context' console.error('[handleRunStage] üö® AI System Not Ready - Detailed Diagnostics:', diagnosticInfo);\n   564‚Üí      \n   565‚Üí      // Determine specific error cause and solution\n   566‚Üí      let     errorTitle = \"AI Module Failed to Load\";\n   572‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system encountered an error during initialization and cannot process \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   573‚Üí
